<h1 class="title pg-title" >
At Least 8 Killed In &#39;Extremely Brutal&#39; Russian Strikes On Kharkiv, Donetsk
</h1>
<div class="cover-media">
<figure class="media-image js-media-expand">
<div class="img-wrap">
<div class="thumb thumb16_9">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-15d4-08dc7b1e4d81_cx0_cy3_cw0_w250_r1_s.jpg" alt="A firefighter works at the site where a printing press was hit by Russian missile strikes in Kharkiv, Ukraine, on May 23." />
</div>
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen ico--media-expand ico--rounded"></span>
</div>
<figcaption>
<span class="caption" data-cms-inline-wrap="caption" data-cms-inline-text="">A firefighter works at the site where a printing press was hit by Russian missile strikes in Kharkiv, Ukraine, on May 23.</span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
</div>
<input class="switcher-controller news__control accordeon__control" id="more-less-32960202" checked type="checkbox" />
<div class="news__buttons news__buttons--main pos-abs">
<button class="btn btn--news btn--news-more pos-abs">
<span class="ico ico-chevron-down"></span>
</button>
<button class="btn btn--news sticky-btn btn--news-less">
<span class="ico ico-close"></span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="wsw accordeon__target">
<p>At least seven people were killed on May 23 in Ukraine's second-largest city of Kharkiv in a <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.radiosvoboda.org/a/news-kharkiv-zahybli/32960543.html" target="_blank">wave</a></strong> of Russian strikes that President Volodymyr Zelenskiy called &quot;extremely brutal&quot; as he again appealed to allies for more air-defense systems for his embattled country.</p>
<p>Ukraine's State Emergency Service <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.facebook.com/MNS.GOV.UA/posts/865004869000737?ref=embed_post" target="_blank">announced the increase</a></strong> in the number of dead and injured on Facebook in a post that included photos of emergency response workers extinguishing a fire and assisting victims.</p>
<p>Oleh Synyehubov, the governor of Ukraine's northeastern Kharkiv region, said earlier on Telegram that Russia launched at least 15 missiles at the city, killing six civilians and wounding another 16, while two more people were still missing after the attack. He said later that seven were killed, including five women.</p><div class="backgrounder content-floated overlap-md ">
<div class="wsw">
<h3 class="wsw__h3">Live Briefing: Russia&#39;s Invasion Of Ukraine</h3>
<div class="wsw__embed">
<figure class="media-image js-media-expand">
<div class="img-wrap">
<div class="thumb">
<img alt="" src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-1cfa-08dc297e7d3d_w250_r0_s.jpg" />
</div>
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen ico--media-expand ico--rounded" />
</div>
</figure>
</div>
<p>RFE/RL's <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.rferl.org/a/ukraine-russia-crisis-crosshairs-live-briefing/31668477.html" target="_blank">Live Briefing</a> </strong>gives you all of the latest developments on Russia's full-scale invasion, Kyiv's counteroffensive, Western military aid, global reaction, and the plight of civilians<em>. </em>For all of RFE/RL's coverage of the war in Ukraine, <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.rferl.org/russia-invades-ukraine" target="_blank">click here</a></strong>.</p> </div>
</div>
<p>&quot;All of them are civilians. All of them are employees of a well-known enterprise that printed magazines, newspapers, and other printing,&quot; <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://t.me/synegubov/9655" target="_blank">he said</a></strong>, adding that about 50 people were working at the time of the strike.</p>
<p>Kharkiv Mayor Ihor Terekhov <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://t.me/ihor_terekhov/1014" target="_blank">said</a></strong> separately that one missile struck a printing press, triggering a large-scale fire.</p>
<p>Russian forces launched a surprise offensive on the Kharkiv region on May 10, shelling border settlements and attempting to capture Vovchansk, a small town just 5 kilometers from the Russian border.</p>
<p>More than 9,000 people have been evacuated from the area, although outgunned and outmanned Ukrainian forces have managed to keep the Russians at bay so far.</p>
<p>Kharkiv, a city of more than 1.4 million before the war, located at some 35 kilometers from the border, has been increasingly subjected to missile and drone attacks as Ukraine's lack of enough modern air-defense systems and ammunition became more evident by the day.</p>
<p>&quot;An extremely brutal Russian attack on Kharkiv and [the nearby town of] Lyubotyn. According to preliminary data, Russia launched 15 missiles at once,&quot; Zelenskiy wrote on X, formerly Twitter.</p>
<p>&quot;Russian terrorists are taking advantage of Ukraine's lack of sufficient air-defense protection and reliable capability to destroy terrorist launchers at their exact locations, which are close to our borders,&quot; Zelenskiy said.</p>
<p>&quot;I am grateful to everyone who is helping us. But we need more determination, especially from world leaders,&quot; he said.</p>
<p>Separately, Donetsk regional Governor Vadym Filashkin <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.radiosvoboda.org/a/news-ova-obstrily-poraneni/32960257.html" target="_blank">said</a></strong> on May 23 that one person was killed and 26 others were wounded in Russian shelling of the town of Toretsk.</p><div data-owner-ct="None" data-inline="False">
<div class="media-block also-read">
<a class="img-wrap img-wrap--size-3 also-read__img" href="/a/ukraine-war-russia-military-recruiting-donbas/32959105.html" title="In Occupied Areas, Russia Pushes Ukrainian Youth To Sign Contracts To Fight Ukraine">
<span class="thumb thumb16_9">
<noscript class="nojs-img">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0a00-0242-d99c-08dc4a737d4d_cx0_cy17_cw0_w100_r1.jpg" alt="Russian soldiers stand near a mobile recruiting center with a board containing information about payments in Rostov-on-Don, Russia.">
</noscript>
<img data-src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0a00-0242-d99c-08dc4a737d4d_cx0_cy17_cw0_w100_r1.jpg" alt="Russian soldiers stand near a mobile recruiting center with a board containing information about payments in Rostov-on-Don, Russia." />
</span>
</a> <div class="media-block__content also-read__body also-read__body--h">
<a href="/a/ukraine-war-russia-military-recruiting-donbas/32959105.html" title="In Occupied Areas, Russia Pushes Ukrainian Youth To Sign Contracts To Fight Ukraine">
<span class="also-read__text--label">
SEE ALSO:
</span>
<h4 class="media-block__title media-block__title--size-3 also-read__text p-0">
In Occupied Areas, Russia Pushes Ukrainian Youth To Sign Contracts To Fight Ukraine
</h4>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>On the Russian side, <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.radiosvoboda.org/a/news-krym-vybukhy/32961202.html" target="_blank">two deaths</a></strong> were reported in occupied Crimea after explosions were heard on the peninsula.<br />
<br />
Sergei Aksyonov, the Moscow-installed governor of Crimea, said on Telegram that a Ukrainian missile attack killed two bystanders near Simferopol, the peninsula's main administrative center. Aksyonov also said a Ukrainian missile struck an empty building near Alushta on the peninsula's Black Sea coast.<br />
<br />
There was no comment on the attack from Ukraine.<br />
<br />
The Russian Defense Ministry, meanwhile, said its air-defense systems repelled a large Ukrainian rocket and drone attack targeting Belgorod region on May 23.</p>
<p>&quot;The air-defense systems on duty destroyed three Vilkha MLRS rockets, 32 Vampire MLRS rockets, and three UAVs over the territory of the Belgorod region,&quot; the ministry said in a <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.rferl.org/a/belgorod-rocket-drone-attack-gladkov/32960202.html" target="_blank">message</a></strong> on Telegram.</p>
<p>Belgorod Governor Cyacheslav Gladkov said in a separate message that there were no casualties from the attack, but two children's camps were damaged by falling debris.</p>
<p>The claims could not be independently verified immediately. Ukraine has not commented.</p>
<p>In a separate development, the Conflict Intelligence Team investigation group said it had <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://notes.citeam.org/ru-dispatch-may-20-22-2024" target="_blank">confirmation</a></strong> that the small Russian small missile corvette Tsiklon (Cyclone) was sunk following a Ukrainian attack on Sevastopol on the night of May 19. The Black Sea Fleet received this ship in the summer of last year.</p>
</div>

<h1 class="title pg-title" >
Norway Slaps Further Restrictions On Russian Visitors
</h1>
<div class="cover-media">
<figure class="media-image js-media-expand">
<div class="img-wrap">
<div class="thumb thumb16_9">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/02a30000-0aff-0242-da91-08da29da7151_cx0_cy7_cw0_w250_r1_s.jpg" alt="Norway-Russia border (file photo)" />
</div>
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen ico--media-expand ico--rounded"></span>
</div>
<figcaption>
<span class="caption" data-cms-inline-wrap="caption" data-cms-inline-text="">Norway-Russia border (file photo)</span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
</div>
<input class="switcher-controller news__control accordeon__control" id="more-less-32960162" checked type="checkbox" />
<div class="news__buttons news__buttons--main pos-abs">
<button class="btn btn--news btn--news-more pos-abs">
<span class="ico ico-chevron-down"></span>
</button>
<button class="btn btn--news sticky-btn btn--news-less">
<span class="ico ico-close"></span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="wsw accordeon__target">
<p>Norway has <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.regjeringen.no/en/aktuelt/restricting-the-possibilities-of-entry-for-russian-citizens/id3040398/" target="_blank">announced</a></strong> further restrictions for the entry of Russian citizens in the Nordic country in reaction to Moscow's ongoing war in Ukraine. Oslo first introduced restrictions on visas for Russian visitors in the spring of 2022, after the start of Russia's unprovoked full-scale invasion. Under the new restrictions, police can refuse the entry of certain Russian citizens, the Justice Ministry said in a statement. &quot;The decision...is in line with the Norwegian approach of standing by allies and partners in the reactions against Russia's illegal war of aggression against Ukraine,&quot; it said. The new rules take effect on May 29.</p>
</div>

<label class="news__read-more-label accordeon__control-label pos-abs" for="more-less-32960162"></label>

<span class="btn__text">

</span>
</a>

<h1 class="title pg-title" >
UN General Assembly To Vote On Resolution To Commemorate Srebrenica Genocide
</h1>
<div class="cover-media">
<figure class="media-image js-media-expand">
<div class="img-wrap">
<div class="thumb thumb16_9">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-f850-08dc7a987aa7_cx0_cy2_cw96_w250_r1_s.jpg" alt="A woman prays amid the gravestones of Srebrenica victims at a memorial cemetery in Potocari. " />
</div>
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen ico--media-expand ico--rounded"></span>
</div>
<figcaption>
<span class="caption" data-cms-inline-wrap="caption" data-cms-inline-text="">A woman prays amid the gravestones of Srebrenica victims at a memorial cemetery in Potocari. </span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
</div>
<input class="switcher-controller news__control accordeon__control" id="more-less-32959682" checked type="checkbox" />
<div class="news__buttons news__buttons--main pos-abs">
<button class="btn btn--news btn--news-more pos-abs">
<span class="ico ico-chevron-down"></span>
</button>
<button class="btn btn--news sticky-btn btn--news-less">
<span class="ico ico-close"></span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="wsw accordeon__target">
<p>The UN General Assembly has scheduled a debate on a UN resolution to establish an annual day to commemorate the 1995 genocide of more than 8,000 Bosnian Muslims by Bosnian Serbs on May 23 to be followed by a vote.</p>
<p>The resolution would designate July 11 as the International Day of Reflection and Commemoration of the 1995 Genocide in Srebrenica.</p>
<p>The resolution has sparked protests and a lobbying campaign by Serbia’s president and the Bosnian Serb leadership to block its adoption by the 193-member General Assembly. Approval requires a majority of those countries that take part in the vote.</p>
<p>The draft resolution condemns “without reservation any denial of the Srebrenica genocide as a historical event.” It also “condemns without reservation actions that glorify those convicted of war crimes, crimes against humanity and genocide by international courts, including those responsible for the Srebrenica genocide.”</p>
<p>Sponsored by Germany and Rwanda, the resolution also asks the United Nations to prepare an outreach program and invites countries, organizations, civil society organizations, and others to observe July 11 with “appropriate education and public awareness-raising activities&quot; in memory and honor of the victims.</p>
<p>The killings began near the end of the 1992-95 Bosnian War, which broke out after the breakup of Yugoslavia and pitted Bosnian Serbs against the country’s two other main ethnic populations, Croats and Muslim Bosniaks.</p><div class="wsw__embed">

<a href="/embed/player/Article/32806254.html?type=video&amp;FullScreenMode=True" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="c-mmp__cpanel-btn c-mmp__cpanel-btn--fullscreen js-btn-fullscreen" title="fullscreen">

<p>On July 11, 1995, Bosnian Serbs overran a UN-protected safe area in Srebrenica and began targeting Bosniak men and boys. Those who tried to escape were chased through the woods and over the mountains around the town.<br />
<br />
The International Court of Justice, the UN’s highest tribunal, determined in 2007 that the acts committed in Srebrenica constituted genocide, and the court’s determination is included in the draft resolution.</p>
<p>Germany’s UN Ambassador Antje Leendertse said the resolution “has the support of a large cross-regional group. She noted in a statement to the Associated Press last week that there is an official UN commemoration of the 1994 Rwanda genocide every year on April 7, and the Srebrenica resolution aims to do the same for Bosnia before the 30th anniversary of the start of the genocide in 2025.</p>
<p>Serbia’s nationalist president, Aleksandar Vucic, and the leadership of the Bosnian Serb entity, Republika Srpska, have vehemently opposed the adoption of the resolution, saying it brands Serbia as a “genocidal nation.”</p>
<p>Serbian Foreign Minister Marko Duric told the UN Security Council on April 30 that Serbia has consistently condemned the “horrific” Srebrenica massacre and other crimes committed during the Bosnian War. Duric called for the resolution to be withdrawn and replaced by one that honors all victims of the war.<br />
<br />
Vucic said the resolution should be subjected to a vote in the UN Security Council, not the General Assembly. Those put to a vote in the Security Council can be vetoed by any of its five members, therefore allowing Russia and China to sink it.</p><div data-owner-ct="None" data-inline="False">
<div class="media-block also-read">
<a class="img-wrap img-wrap--size-3 also-read__img" href="/a/bosnia-textbooks-war-serbia-veterans-biased-narratives/32889283.html" title="War Veterans In Bosnia Are Angry About How The War Is Being Taught">
<span class="thumb thumb16_9">
<noscript class="nojs-img">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-b44f-08dc4cd4311e_w100_r1.png" alt="Schoolchildren in Bosnia-Herzegovina have long been taught a sanitized version of the terrible tragedies of the 1990s, largely to avoid biased narratives. A Serb veterans’ group is trying to change that. (photo illustration)">
</noscript>
<img data-src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-b44f-08dc4cd4311e_w100_r1.png" alt="Schoolchildren in Bosnia-Herzegovina have long been taught a sanitized version of the terrible tragedies of the 1990s, largely to avoid biased narratives. A Serb veterans’ group is trying to change that. (photo illustration)" />
</span>
</a> <div class="media-block__content also-read__body also-read__body--h">
<a href="/a/bosnia-textbooks-war-serbia-veterans-biased-narratives/32889283.html" title="War Veterans In Bosnia Are Angry About How The War Is Being Taught">
<span class="also-read__text--label">
SEE ALSO:
</span>
<h4 class="media-block__title media-block__title--size-3 also-read__text p-0">
War Veterans In Bosnia Are Angry About How The War Is Being Taught
</h4>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Russia’s envoy to the UN, Vasily Nebenzya, dismissed the resolution as “one-sided” and “politically charged” in his comments to the Security Council on April 30. Nebenzya said the move would not promote reconciliation among the peoples of Bosnia-Herzegovina.</p>
<p>Milorad Dodik, Republika Srpska's Russia-friendly leader, has repeatedly threatened that if the resolution is adopted, the entity &quot;will withdraw from the decision-making process in Bosnia.&quot;<br />
<br />
Dodik, who has regularly reiterated his denial of the Srebrenica genocide, told supporters at a rally in Banja Luka last month that the actions of the Republika Srpska Army in Srebrenica in 1995 were &quot;a mistake that left the crime,&quot; but he denied it was genocide.</p>
<h6 class="wsw__h6">With reporting by AP</h6>
</div>

<h1 class="title pg-title" >
Turkey Claims Its Drone Was Instrumental In Finding Wreckage Of Iranian Helicopter
</h1>
<div class="cover-media">
<figure class="media-image js-media-expand">
<div class="img-wrap">
<div class="thumb thumb16_9">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/4f19a5be-3e75-4bf4-b4cc-c7f086fddfd6_cx4_cy8_cw84_w250_r1_s.jpg" alt="An Akinci drone made by Turkey (file photo)" />
</div>
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen ico--media-expand ico--rounded"></span>
</div>
<figcaption>
<span class="caption" data-cms-inline-wrap="caption" data-cms-inline-text="">An Akinci drone made by Turkey (file photo)</span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
</div>
<input class="switcher-controller news__control accordeon__control" id="more-less-32959633" checked type="checkbox" />
<div class="news__buttons news__buttons--main pos-abs">
<button class="btn btn--news btn--news-more pos-abs">
<span class="ico ico-chevron-down"></span>
</button>
<button class="btn btn--news sticky-btn btn--news-less">
<span class="ico ico-close"></span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="wsw accordeon__target">
<p>Turkey says its Akinci drone deserves more credit for helping to locate the wreckage of the Iranian helicopter that crashed in a remote and mountainous area of Iran on May 19, killing President Ebrahim Raisi and other top Iranian officials, according to Turkish media reports on May 22.</p>
<p>The reports say that the <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.radiofarda.com/a/32957819.html" target="_blank">Akinci drone</a></strong> was first to find the site of the wreckage and accused Iran of changing its narrative about the use of the Turkish equipment after it provided information about the location of the wreckage and then made counterclaims that its own drone found the site.</p>
<p>Turkish President Recep Tayyip Erdogan said earlier this week that the Akinci drone was sent at the request of the Iranian government.</p>
<p>According to Erdogan, despite the bad weather conditions the drone was able to conduct search operations in the region for seven and a half hours and fly a total of 2,100 kilometers.</p>
<p>After the Turkish drone identified the helicopter wreckage and detected heat sources believed to be the crash site in Iran’s East Azerbaijan Province, the Iranian search team successfully located the downed helicopter and the bodies of Raisi and the others in the mountainous terrain, according to Turkish media reports.</p>
<p>However, Iran rejected the notion that there was foreign participation in the search operation despite data from the Turkish drone that revealed the coordinates of the crash, and confirmation of this data by some Iranian news agencies.</p>
<p>After the Akinci drone captured images of the wreckage using its night vision and thermal camera and released them on the Internet, Pirhossein Kolivand, the head of the Iranian Red Crescent Society, called foreign participation in the search a rumor.</p>
<p>“We did not stop the search in the dark, fog, and rain, and when we discovered the wreckage of the helicopter with our own drone, we moved to the exact place where the helicopter fell,&quot; Kolivand said.</p>
<p>He claimed that rescuers from the Red Crescent found the wreckage at an altitude of 2,500 meters and &quot;it took 40 minutes from the time of finding the wreckage of the helicopter to reaching the accident site.”</p><div class="wsw__embed">
<div class="media-pholder media-pholder--video ">
<div class="c-sticky-container" data-poster="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-d77b-08dc7aa87770_w250_r1.jpg">

<a href="/embed/player/Article/32959421.html?type=video&amp;FullScreenMode=True" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="c-mmp__cpanel-btn c-mmp__cpanel-btn--fullscreen js-btn-fullscreen" title="fullscreen">
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen m-0"></span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>But during the overnight search, the Red Crescent said in a statement at around 4 a.m. local time on May 20 that after the Turkish drone identified two potential “hot spots” the Red Crescent rescue teams headed toward the sites.</p>
<p>The head of the East Azerbaijan Red Crescent also cited the Turkish drone report that a “burning spot” had been detected and said rescue forces were sent to that area.</p>
<p>The head of Turkey, Asia, and Indo-Pacific studies at the Institute for International Relations and Strategic Research (ULISA) said in an opinion piece published by the state news agency Anadolu that the drone’s role in finding the wreckage site demonstrated the need to recognize Turkey’s commitment to fulfilling its humanitarian responsibilities through its defense capacity.</p>
<p>Professor M. Nazmul Islam said that, after Iran accepted Turkey’s offer to send the drone, the Akinci took off from a Turkish base at around 11:30 p.m. local time and began searching nearly an hour later. Turkey claims that it transmitted the image of the wreckage of the helicopter at 3:06 a.m. Iranian time and shared the coordinates with the Iranian authorities.</p>
<p>But according to Iranian media accounts, an Iranian drone belonging to the Quds Force of the Islamic Revolutionary Guards Corps found the remains of the helicopter at around 5:30 a.m. local time.</p>
<p>A statement issued by Iran's military said that, despite Turkey sending a drone equipped with night vision and thermal cameras, it &quot;failed to accurately locate the crash site due to its lack of detection equipment and control points below the cloud,&quot; referring to the adverse weather conditions.</p>
<p>Iran Radio reported that it was “five o'clock in the morning when the correct coordinates were finally found with Iranian equipment and Iranian relief forces.”</p>
<p>Iran, whose military has its own drone program, was not able to deploy its drones because they were located in the northern part of the Indian Ocean at the time, the Iranian military said. Western powers have accused Iran of providing drones to Russia for its war in Ukraine.</p>
<h6 class="wsw__h6">With reporting by Anadolu and Reuters</h6>
</div>

<h1 class="title pg-title" >
Bulgarian Prosecutor Seeks Closure Of 2 Pro-Russian Paramilitary Groups
</h1>
<div class="cover-media">
<figure class="media-image js-media-expand">
<div class="img-wrap">
<div class="thumb thumb16_9">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-aaca-08db59f2568f_w250_r1_s.jpg" alt="Pro-Russian demonstrators hold a rally in Sofia in May 2023." />
</div>
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen ico--media-expand ico--rounded"></span>
</div>
<figcaption>
<span class="caption" data-cms-inline-wrap="caption" data-cms-inline-text="">Pro-Russian demonstrators hold a rally in Sofia in May 2023.</span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
</div>
<input class="switcher-controller news__control accordeon__control" id="more-less-32959539" checked type="checkbox" />
<div class="news__buttons news__buttons--main pos-abs">
<button class="btn btn--news btn--news-more pos-abs">
<span class="ico ico-chevron-down"></span>
</button>
<button class="btn btn--news sticky-btn btn--news-less">
<span class="ico ico-close"></span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="wsw accordeon__target">
<p class="x">Two pro-Russian paramilitary organizations operating in Bulgaria should be closed because their activities violate the constitution, a district prosecutor’s office said on May 22.</p>
<p class="x">The request to shut down BNO Shipka and the Vasil Levski Military Union was <a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.svobodnaevropa.bg/a/prokuraturata-iska-zakrivane-bno-shipka-voinski-saiuz-vasil-levski/32959351.html" target="_blank"><strong>submitted</strong> </a>to the district court in Varna by the local prosecutor’s office. The court is expected to schedule a hearing to consider the request.</p>
<p class="x">The two paramilitary organizations are connected to one another and known for their pro-Russian rhetoric. They have been conducting combat training for years and oppose Bulgaria’s Euro-Atlantic affiliations, including its membership in the European Union and in NATO.</p>
<p class="x">The request comes a year and a half after the state prosecutor’s office announced that it was investigating BNO Shipka for sedition.</p>
<p class="x">Investigators found that the two paramilitary organizations violated the constitution’s prohibition of actions “against the sovereignty [and] territorial integrity of the country and the unity of the nation” and its prohibition of inciting hatred and creating &quot;secret or paramilitary structures.&quot;</p>
<p class="x">The Varna district prosecutor's office said members of both groups had made organized visits to the border with Turkey aimed at &quot;catching illegal migrants.&quot;</p>
<p class="x">In addition, the leaders of the two associations have maintained contacts with representatives of German political factions, including people known for their far-right beliefs, the investigators said.</p>
<p class="x">The groups describe their activities as patriotic.</p>
<p class="x">The leader and spokesman for the organizations, a man who introduces himself as Vladimir Rusev, has spread conspiracy theories against NATO and the European Union on social media for years. Rusev, who has gained fame in the past with the nickname Walter Kalashnikov, opposes COVID-19 vaccination, linking it to disinformation that circulated on social media during the pandemic.</p>
<p class="x">Questions about the organizations were raised last year by investigative journalist Hristo Grozev, who reported that they were linked to a 2016 attempt by Russia to destabilize Bulgaria using a model deployed in Montenegro the same year.</p>
<p class="x">Grozev’s investigation looked into a protest in Sofia in April 2016 organized by BNO Shipka and the Vasil Levski Military Union in front of the National Assembly. Many of the activists of the paramilitary organizations were preemptively detained before the protest.</p>
<p class="x">A few months later members of the organizations beat protesters who demonstrated against the visit of the pro-Russian biker Night Wolves club to the Black Sea port city of Burgas. The Burgas district court in April 2019 convicted three people in the case.</p>
</div>

<h1 class="title pg-title" >
Custody Extended For Russian Teen Jailed For Posting Ukrainian Poet
</h1>
<div class="cover-media">
<figure class="media-image js-media-expand">
<div class="img-wrap">
<div class="thumb thumb16_9">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-4d71-08dc3777618f_cx19_cy17_cw67_w250_r1_s.jpg" alt="Darya Kozyreva in court earlier this year" />
</div>
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen ico--media-expand ico--rounded"></span>
</div>
<figcaption>
<span class="caption" data-cms-inline-wrap="caption" data-cms-inline-text="">Darya Kozyreva in court earlier this year</span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
</div>
<input class="switcher-controller news__control accordeon__control" id="more-less-32959381" checked type="checkbox" />
<div class="news__buttons news__buttons--main pos-abs">
<button class="btn btn--news btn--news-more pos-abs">
<span class="ico ico-chevron-down"></span>
</button>
<button class="btn btn--news sticky-btn btn--news-less">
<span class="ico ico-close"></span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="wsw accordeon__target">
<p>ST. PETERSBURG, Russia -- A court in St. Petersburg has <a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.severreal.org/a/v-peterburge-aktivistku-arestovali-po-delu-o-povtornoy-diskreditatsii-armii-/32836787.html" target="_blank"><strong>extended</strong> </a>pretrial detention by another two months for an 18-year-old activist who is charged with repeatedly discrediting Russian armed forces involved in Moscow’s ongoing invasion of Ukraine.</p>
<p>The Petrograd district court ruled on May 22 that Darya Kozyreva must stay in pretrial detention at least until July 25.</p>
<p>Kozyreva was detained on February 24, the second anniversary of Russia's full-scale invasion of Ukraine, after she glued a poster on a monument to prominent Ukrainian writer, poet, and thinker Taras Shevchenko with an excerpt of a well-known poem from his book, <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://shevchenko.ca/taras-shevchenko/poem.cfm?poem=3" target="_blank">My Testament</a></strong>:</p>
<p style="margin-left:40px; text-align:justify"><em>Oh bury me, then rise ye up</em></p>
<p style="margin-left:40px; text-align:justify"><em>And break your heavy chains</em></p>
<p style="margin-left:40px; text-align:justify"><em>And water with the tyrants' blood </em></p>
<p style="margin-left:40px; text-align:justify"><em>The freedom you have gained.</em></p>
<p>The poster was so strongly glued to the monument that police were unable to remove it and had to cover it with a black plastic bag.<br />
<br />
Kozyreva was initially charged with vandalism in January last year after she left a comment in December 2022 on an art installation symbolizing &quot;friendship&quot; between St. Petersburg and Ukraine's city of Mariupol, which was destroyed by Russian bombs at the start of the invasion.</p>
<p>An investigation into that case is still under way.<br />
<br />
On December 18, 2022, less than a week after the installation was unveiled in St. Petersburg's Palace Square, the words “Murderers, you bombed it to ruins yourselves!&quot; <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.rferl.org/a/russia-petersburg-mariupol-art-installation-vandalized/32183673.html" target="_blank">appeared</a></strong> on the installation.<br />
<br />
Kozyreva was expelled from St. Petersburg State University in January after she was found guilty of discrediting Russia's armed forces and ordered to pay a 30,000 ruble ($330) fine in December.<br />
<br />
That charge stemmed from Kozyreva's online posts criticizing Russian laws on discrediting the country's armed forces, which were introduced shortly after Russia launched its full-scale invasion in late February 2022.</p>
</div>

<label class="news__read-more-label accordeon__control-label pos-abs" for="more-less-32959381"></label>

<h1 class="title pg-title" >
6 Kyrgyz, 4 Foreign Nationals Detained Over Mob Attacks In Bishkek
</h1>
<div class="cover-media">
<figure class="media-image js-media-expand">
<div class="img-wrap">
<div class="thumb thumb16_9">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-06b5-08dc795ba94e_w250_r1_s.jpg" alt="Pakistani students leaving Kyrgyzstan following mob attacks. Manas international airport in Bishkek. May 21, 2024" />
</div>
<span class="ico ico-fullscreen ico--media-expand ico--rounded"></span>
</div>
<figcaption>
<span class="caption" data-cms-inline-wrap="caption" data-cms-inline-text="">Pakistani students leaving Kyrgyzstan following mob attacks. Manas international airport in Bishkek. May 21, 2024</span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
</div>
<input class="switcher-controller news__control accordeon__control" id="more-less-32959434" checked type="checkbox" />
<div class="news__buttons news__buttons--main pos-abs">
<button class="btn btn--news btn--news-more pos-abs">
<span class="ico ico-chevron-down"></span>
</button>
<button class="btn btn--news sticky-btn btn--news-less">
<span class="ico ico-close"></span>
</button>
</div>
<div class="wsw accordeon__target">
<p>BISHKEK -- The Kyrgyz Interior Ministry <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.azattyk.org/a/32959010.html" target="_blank">said</a></strong> on May 22 that six Kyrgyz and four foreign citizens had been detained on suspicion of being involved in a brawl that sparked mob attacks on foreign students in Bishkek, triggering a mass exodus of Pakistani students from the Central Asian nation.</p>
<p>According to the ministry, nine investigations have been launched into hooliganism, robbery, mass disorder, and inciting ethnic hatred. Thirty-three people were injured in the violence, the ministry added.</p>
<p>Hundreds of Pakistani students have left Kyrgyzstan since the May 18 violence, which was triggered by the appearance on social media of a video purportedly showing a group of &quot;people of Asian appearance&quot; harassing foreign students on the night of May 13.</p><div class="wsw__embed">

<a href="/embed/player/Article/32959335.html?type=video&amp;FullScreenMode=True" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="c-mmp__cpanel-btn c-mmp__cpanel-btn--fullscreen js-btn-fullscreen" title="fullscreen">

<p>The group then pursued the students to their dormitory, where at least one foreigner was assaulted by several men and dragged along the floor.</p>
<p>Kyrgyz officials said later that the foreigners involved in the brawl on video were Egyptians.</p>
<p>The Kyrgyz government has vowed to pursue those responsible for the violence.</p>
<p>Still, it appeared to lay the blame for the attack on illegal migrants, saying authorities had been taking &quot;decisive measures to suppress illegal migration and expel undesirable persons from Kyrgyzstan.&quot;</p>
<p>On May 22, Kyrgyzstan’s State Committee for National Security (UKMK) <strong><a class="wsw__a" href="https://www.azattyk.org/a/32959077.html" target="_blank">said</a></strong> in a statement that five Egyptian citizens were arrested on charges of extortion, illegal drug possession, and violating immigration laws.</p><div data-owner-ct="None" data-inline="False">
<div class="media-block also-read">
<a class="img-wrap img-wrap--size-3 also-read__img" href="/a/mass-labor-kyrgyzstan-migrant-worker-fear/32957992.html" title="Why Mass Labor Exporter Kyrgyzstan Faces Migrant Worker Fear At Home">
<span class="thumb thumb16_9">
<noscript class="nojs-img">
<img src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-8eaf-08dc31102cfc_cx0_cy0_cw71_w100_r1.jpg" alt="South Asian migrant workers in Kyrgyzstan">
</noscript>
<img data-src="https://gdb.rferl.org/01000000-0aff-0242-8eaf-08dc31102cfc_cx0_cy0_cw71_w100_r1.jpg" alt="South Asian migrant workers in Kyrgyzstan" />
</span>
</a> <div class="media-block__content also-read__body also-read__body--h">
<a href="/a/mass-labor-kyrgyzstan-migrant-worker-fear/32957992.html" title="Why Mass Labor Exporter Kyrgyzstan Faces Migrant Worker Fear At Home">
<span class="also-read__text--label">
SEE ALSO:
</span>
<h4 class="media-block__title media-block__title--size-3 also-read__text p-0">
Why Mass Labor Exporter Kyrgyzstan Faces Migrant Worker Fear At Home
</h4>
</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>A day earlier, the UKMK said six Pakistani nationals were detained overnight while trying to illegally enter Kyrgyzstan from Kazakhstan.</p>
<p>Just three days before the violence, the UKMK detained 28 Pakistani nationals for &quot;working illegally&quot; in a sewing shop in Bishkek.</p>
<p>The same day, Bishkek city police shut down delivery services conducted by more than 400 foreign students, mostly from Pakistan, on motorcycles and scooters, citing traffic safety concerns.</p>
</div>
